## Interpretation
- Prefer moving content into `hfo_hot_obsidian_forge/` or `hfo_cold_obsidian_forge/`.
- For load-bearing legacy paths, convert call-sites to resolve via `hfo_pointers.py`.
- Keep `hfo_hot_obsidian/` and `hfo_cold_obsidian/` as compatibility-only drains until cutover is complete.
